layout: "post"
title: "The circle"
date: "2018-05-01"
agda: true
toc: true
categories: type-theory
---

In this entry, we want to show some equivalences
between the circle and other higher inductive types.

{% comment %}

{: . equation }

  $$\sum\,{\mathbb{S}^1}\,(\mathsf{rec}_{\mathbb{S}^1}\, \mathcal{U}\,  2\,
  (\mathsf{ua}(\mathsf{rec}_{2}2 1_{2} 0_{2}))) \simeq \mathbb{S}^1.$$

I gave a talk giving one solution using the flattening lemma:

- [**Direct link PDF**](https://github.com/jonaprieto/flattenlem/files/2045561/Jonathan-Prieto-Cubides-The-Flattening-Lemma.pdf)

{% endcomment %}

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="616" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="621" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="628" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}" class="Module">2018-07-06-mini-hott</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

##  S¹ type

The circle is the higher inductive type with one point
and one no trivial path called path as we show in the following
picture.

![path](/assets/ipe-images/circle.png)
*Figure 1. The circle type `S¹`.*

## `pS` type

![path](/assets/ipe-images/tour-type.png)
*Figure 2. `pS` Type.*

## Equivalences

### Lemma 1

{: .equation }

  $$ \mathsf{S}^{1} \simeq \mathsf{pS}. $$

**Proof**.

Let us define the outgoing functions:

The proof of the homotopy $$ f' ∘ g' \sim \mathsf{id}$$.

          <a id="8388" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#5179" class="Function">refl</a> <a id="8393" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#2058" class="Function">pS₀</a>
        <a id="8405" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#7901" class="Function Operator">∎</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The proof of the homotopy $$g' ∘ f' \sim \mathsf{id}$$:

### Lemma 2

- Action on paths of pairs

### Lemma 3

{: .equation}
  $$
    \Sigma~S^{1}~P~\simeq~pS
  $$

  where $$P (\mathsf{base}) :≡ \mathsf{Bool}$$ and $$\mathsf{ap~P~loop~=~ua~(neg)}$$.

            <a id="13640" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#7802" class="Function Operator">==⟨</a> <a id="13644" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#23742" class="Function">funext</a> <a id="13651" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="13654" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13655" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13655" class="Bound">pb</a> <a id="13658" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13660" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#11902" class="Function">P</a> <a id="13662" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#961" class="Function">base</a><a id="13666" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13668" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13670" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#8179" class="Function">ap</a> <a id="13673" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#12983" class="Function">d̰</a> <a id="13676" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13677" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#12293" class="Function">aux-lemma₁</a> <a id="13688" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13655" class="Bound">pb</a><a id="13690" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="13693" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#7802" class="Function Operator">⟩</a>
          <a id="13705" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="13708" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13709" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13709" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="13711" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13713" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#11902" class="Function">P</a> <a id="13715" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#961" class="Function">base</a><a id="13719" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13721" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13723" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#12983" class="Function">d̰</a> <a id="13726" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13727" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#11724" class="Function">neg</a> <a id="13731" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13709" class="Bound">x</a><a id="13732" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13734" class="Symbol">)</a>
            <a id="13748" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#7802" class="Function Operator">==⟨</a> <a id="13752" class="Symbol">{!   !}</a>  <a id="13761" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#7802" class="Function Operator">⟩</a> <a id="13763" class="Comment">-- I got stuck here.</a>
          <a id="13794" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#12983" class="Function">d̰</a>
         <a id="13806" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#7901" class="Function Operator">∎</a>

<a id="13809" class="Comment">-- ΣSP-≃-pS : Σ S¹ P ≃ pS</a>
<a id="13835" class="Comment">-- ΣSP-≃-pS = qinv-≃ f {!   !}</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="13893" class="Comment">-- -- Defs.</a>
<a id="13905" class="Comment">--     γ₀₁   = transport-ua P loop neg-eq (S¹-βrec Type₀ Bool (ua neg-eq)) false</a>
<a id="13986" class="Comment">--     g-p₀₁ = pair= (loop , γ₀₁)</a>
<a id="14020" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="14023" class="Comment">--     γ₁₀   = transport-ua P loop neg-eq (S¹-βrec Type₀ Bool (ua neg-eq)) true</a>
<a id="14103" class="Comment">--     g-p₁₀ = pair= (loop , γ₁₀)</a>
<a id="14137" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="14140" class="Comment">--     g : pS → Σ S¹ P</a>
<a id="14163" class="Comment">--     g = -- 0   ↦ (base, 0)</a>
<a id="14193" class="Comment">--         -- 1   ↦ (base, 1)</a>
<a id="14223" class="Comment">--         -- p₀₁ ↦ (base, 0) == (base, 1)</a>
<a id="14266" class="Comment">--         -- p₁₀ ↦ (base, 1) == (base, 0)</a>
<a id="14309" class="Comment">--         pS-rec</a>
<a id="14327" class="Comment">--             (Σ S¹ P)</a>
<a id="14351" class="Comment">--             (base , false)</a>
<a id="14381" class="Comment">--             (base , true)</a>
<a id="14410" class="Comment">--             g-p₀₁</a>
<a id="14431" class="Comment">--             g-p₁₀</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="14477" class="Comment">-- -- Missing lemmas.</a>
<a id="14499" class="Comment">--     postulate</a>
<a id="14516" class="Comment">--       lemma-ap-f-γ₀₁ : ap f (pair= (loop , γ₀₁)) == p₀₁</a>
<a id="14575" class="Comment">--       lemma-ap-f-γ₁₀ : ap f (pair= (loop , γ₁₀)) == p₁₀</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Let us prove the homotopies:
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="14688" class="Comment">-- Homotopy</a>
    <a id="14704" class="Comment">-- f-g : f ∘ g ∼ id</a>
    <a id="14728" class="Comment">-- f-g = pS-ind (λ ps → (f ∘ g) ps == id ps) q₀ q₁ dpath₁ dpath₂</a>
    <a id="14797" class="Comment">--   where</a>
    <a id="14812" class="Comment">--</a>
    <a id="14819" class="Comment">--     q₀ : (f ∘ g) pS₀ == id pS₀</a>
    <a id="14857" class="Comment">--     q₀ = p₀₁</a>
    <a id="14877" class="Comment">--</a>
    <a id="14884" class="Comment">--     q₁ : (f ∘ g) pS₁ == id pS₁</a>
    <a id="14922" class="Comment">--     q₁ = p₀₁</a>
    <a id="14942" class="Comment">--</a>
    <a id="14949" class="Comment">--     dpath₁ :  q₀ == q₁ [ (λ z → (f ∘ g) z == id z) ↓ p₀₁ ]</a>
    <a id="15015" class="Comment">--     dpath₁ =</a>
    <a id="15035" class="Comment">--       begin</a>
    <a id="15054" class="Comment">--         transport (λ z → (f ∘ g) z == id z) p₀₁ q₀</a>
    <a id="15112" class="Comment">--           ==⟨ transport-eq-fun (f ∘ g) id p₀₁ q₀ ⟩</a>
    <a id="15170" class="Comment">--         ! ap (f ∘ g) p₀₁ · q₀ · ap id p₀₁</a>
    <a id="15219" class="Comment">--           ==⟨ ap (! ap (f ∘ g) p₀₁ · q₀ ·_) (ap-id p₀₁) ⟩</a>
    <a id="15284" class="Comment">--         ! ap (f ∘ g) p₀₁ · q₀ · p₀₁</a>
    <a id="15327" class="Comment">--           ==⟨ ap (λ r → ! r · q₀ · p₀₁) (! ap-comp g f p₀₁) ⟩</a>
    <a id="15396" class="Comment">--         ! ap f (ap g p₀₁) · q₀ · p₀₁</a>
    <a id="15440" class="Comment">--           ==⟨ ap (λ r → ! ap f r · q₀ · p₀₁)</a>
    <a id="15492" class="Comment">--                  (pS-βrec₀₁ ((Σ S¹ (λ b → P b))) (base , false) (base , true) g-p₀₁ g-p₁₀) ⟩</a>
    <a id="15592" class="Comment">--         ! ap f g-p₀₁ · q₀ · p₀₁</a>
    <a id="15631" class="Comment">--           ==⟨ ap (λ r → ! r · q₀ · p₀₁) lemma-ap-f-γ₀₁ ⟩</a>
    <a id="15695" class="Comment">--         ! p₁₀ · q₀ · p₀₁</a>
    <a id="15727" class="Comment">--           ==⟨⟩</a>
    <a id="15749" class="Comment">--         ! p₁₀ · p₁₀ · p₀₁</a>
    <a id="15782" class="Comment">--           ==⟨ ap (_· p₀₁) (·-linv p₁₀) ⟩</a>
    <a id="15830" class="Comment">--         idp · p₀₁</a>
    <a id="15855" class="Comment">--           ==⟨ ·-lunit p₀₁ ⟩</a>
    <a id="15890" class="Comment">--         q₁</a>
    <a id="15908" class="Comment">--       ∎</a>
    <a id="15923" class="Comment">--</a>
    <a id="15930" class="Comment">--     dpath₂ : q₁ == q₀ [ (λ z → (f ∘ g) z == id z) ↓ p₁₀ ]</a>
    <a id="15995" class="Comment">--     dpath₂ =</a>
    <a id="16015" class="Comment">--       begin</a>
    <a id="16034" class="Comment">--         transport (λ z → (f ∘ g) z == id z) p₁₀ q₁</a>
    <a id="16092" class="Comment">--           ==⟨ transport-eq-fun (f ∘ g) id p₁₀ q₁ ⟩</a>
    <a id="16150" class="Comment">--         ! ap (f ∘ g) p₁₀ · q₁ · ap id p₁₀</a>
    <a id="16199" class="Comment">--           ==⟨ ap (! ap (f ∘ g) p₁₀ · q₁ ·_) (ap-id p₁₀) ⟩</a>
    <a id="16264" class="Comment">--         ! ap (f ∘ g) p₁₀ · q₁ · p₁₀</a>
    <a id="16307" class="Comment">--           ==⟨ ap (λ r → ! r · q₁ · p₁₀) (! ap-comp g f p₁₀) ⟩</a>
    <a id="16376" class="Comment">--         ! ap f (ap g p₁₀) · q₁ · p₁₀</a>
    <a id="16420" class="Comment">--           ==⟨ ap (λ r → ! ap f r · q₁ · p₁₀)</a>
    <a id="16472" class="Comment">--                  (pS-βrec₁₀ ((Σ S¹ (λ b → P b))) (base , false) (base , true) g-p₀₁ g-p₁₀) ⟩</a>
    <a id="16572" class="Comment">--         ! ap f g-p₁₀ · q₁ · p₁₀</a>
    <a id="16611" class="Comment">--           ==⟨ ap (λ r → ! r · q₁ · p₁₀) lemma-ap-f-γ₁₀ ⟩</a>
    <a id="16675" class="Comment">--         ! p₀₁ · q₁ · p₁₀</a>
    <a id="16707" class="Comment">--           ==⟨⟩</a>
    <a id="16729" class="Comment">--         ! p₀₁ · p₀₁ · p₁₀</a>
    <a id="16762" class="Comment">--           ==⟨ ap (_· p₁₀) (·-linv p₀₁) ⟩</a>
    <a id="16810" class="Comment">--         idp · p₁₀</a>
    <a id="16835" class="Comment">--           ==⟨ ·-lunit p₁₀ ⟩</a>
    <a id="16870" class="Comment">--         q₀</a>
    <a id="16888" class="Comment">--       ∎</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="16924" class="Comment">-- -- Homotopy</a>
<a id="16939" class="Comment">--     g-f : g ∘ f ∼ id</a>
<a id="16963" class="Comment">--     g-f (s , pₛ) = g-f&#39; s pₛ</a>
<a id="16995" class="Comment">--       where</a>
<a id="17010" class="Comment">--         g-f&#39; : (s : S¹) → (pₛ : P s) → (g ∘ f) (s , pₛ) == id (s , pₛ)</a>
<a id="17084" class="Comment">--         g-f&#39; = S¹-ind (λ s → (pₛ : P s) → (g ∘ f) (s , pₛ) == id (s , pₛ)) qb qpath</a>
<a id="17171" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="17174" class="Comment">--           where</a>
<a id="17193" class="Comment">--           qb : (pₛ₁ : P base) → (g ∘ f) (base , pₛ₁) == id (base , pₛ₁)</a>
<a id="17268" class="Comment">--           qb true  = g-p₀₁</a>
<a id="17298" class="Comment">--           qb false = g-p₁₀</a>
<a id="17328" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="17331" class="Comment">--           qpath : qb == qb [(λ z → (pₛ₁ : P z) → (g ∘ f) (z , pₛ₁) == id (z , pₛ₁)) ↓ loop ]</a>
<a id="17427" class="Comment">--           qpath =</a>
<a id="17448" class="Comment">--             begin</a>
<a id="17469" class="Comment">--               transport (λ z → (pₛ₁ : P z) → (g ∘ f) (z , pₛ₁) == id (z , pₛ₁)) loop qb</a>
<a id="17560" class="Comment">--                 ==⟨ {!   !}  ⟩</a>
<a id="17594" class="Comment">--               qb</a>
<a id="17614" class="Comment">--             ∎</a>{% endraw %}</pre>
